<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переодеть.html>переоде́ть</a> (21364)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:одеть.html>оде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переодеть.html>переоде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereodétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">переодева́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change someone's clothes
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>она́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переодеть.html>переоде́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:девочка.html>де́вочку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:белый.html>бе́лое</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>пла́тье</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oná <b>pereodéla</b> dévočku v béloje plátʹje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">she changed the girl's dress for a white one</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to disguise <i>(smb)</i></li>
<li>to change <i>(smth)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переодеть.html>переоде́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:платье.html>пла́тье</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:юбка.html>ю́бку</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereodétʹ</b> plátʹje (júbku)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to change one's dress (skirt)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переодеться.html>переоде́ться</a> (7228)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переодеть.html>переоде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereodétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переодеться.html>переоде́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereodétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переодеваться.html>переодева́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to change (clothing)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переодеть.html>переоде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereodétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***переоценивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переоценивать.html>переоце́нивать</a> (26352)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pereocenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценивать.html>переоце́нивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereocénivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to revalue, to reappraise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценивать.html>переоце́нивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ценность.html>це́нности</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereocénivatʹ</b> cénnosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reappraise old values</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to overestimate, to overrate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценивать.html>переоце́нивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereocénivatʹ</b> svoí síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">overestimate/overrate one's abilities; bite off more than one can chew</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a> (25224)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">пере-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pere-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оценить.html>оцени́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ocenítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pereocenítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценивать.html>переоце́нивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to revalue, to reappraise</li>
<li>to overestimate, to overrate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>pereocenítʹ</b> svoí síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">overestimate/overrate one's abilities; bite off more than one can chew</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трудно.html>тру́дно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:переоценить.html>переоцени́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:факт.html>фа́кта</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">trúdno <b>pereocenítʹ</b> značénije étovo fákta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the importance of this fact can scarcely be overestimated/exaggerated</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:перепад.html>перепа́д</a> (20221)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепад.html>перепа́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perepád</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепад.html>перепа́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепад.html>перепа́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:перепад.html>перепа́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>differential, difference, drop

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">perepisátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:переписывать.html>перепи́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rewrite, to retype

<li>to copy</li>
<li>to make a list, to take a census <i>(of)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всех</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perepisátʹ</b> vsex</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take down (register) everybody's names</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reregister
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переписать.html>переписа́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>perepisátʹ</b> dom na sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reregister a house to one's own name</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переписывать.html>перепи́сывавший</a></b>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:переписываться.html>перепи́сываться</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a.
